void AUSM\+\_\+\+Flux (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int \&}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{_flux_8h_a51243b161eea5261235c049939418205_a51243b161eea5261235c049939418205}\index{Flux.h@{Flux.h}!Calculate\_Face\_Average\_Flux@{Calculate\_Face\_Average\_Flux}}
\index{Calculate\_Face\_Average\_Flux@{Calculate\_Face\_Average\_Flux}!Flux.h@{Flux.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Calculate\_Face\_Average\_Flux()}{Calculate\_Face\_Average\_Flux()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_flux_8h_a51243b161eea5261235c049939418205_a51243b161eea5261235c049939418205} 
void Calculate\+\_\+\+Face\+\_\+\+Average\+\_\+\+Flux (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int \&}]{Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{const int \&}]{N\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{const int \&}]{Face\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{bool}]{Is\+\_\+\+Wall\+\_\+\+Face}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculates the average convective flux at a given face of a cell. 

This function computes the average flux at the interface between two cells using the left and right state variables. It also accounts for wall boundary conditions if the face is a wall face. The flux is calculated based on the velocity, pressure, and density of the cells, as well as the face geometry.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Cell\+\_\+\+No} & Index of the current cell (left cell). \\
\hline
{\em N\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No} & Index of the neighboring cell (right cell). \\
\hline
{\em Face\+\_\+\+No} & Index of the face for which the flux is being calculated. \\
\hline
{\em Is\+\_\+\+Wall\+\_\+\+Face} & Boolean flag indicating whether the face is a wall face. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{_flux_8h_a37aa1bf90adb13316e2746f79d10d124_a37aa1bf90adb13316e2746f79d10d124}\index{Flux.h@{Flux.h}!Calculate\_Flux\_For\_All\_Faces@{Calculate\_Flux\_For\_All\_Faces}}
\index{Calculate\_Flux\_For\_All\_Faces@{Calculate\_Flux\_For\_All\_Faces}!Flux.h@{Flux.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Calculate\_Flux\_For\_All\_Faces()}{Calculate\_Flux\_For\_All\_Faces()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_flux_8h_a37aa1bf90adb13316e2746f79d10d124_a37aa1bf90adb13316e2746f79d10d124} 
void Calculate\+\_\+\+Flux\+\_\+\+For\+\_\+\+All\+\_\+\+Faces (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int \&}]{Current\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{void(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{Dissipation\+\_\+\+Function~}{)(const int \&, int \&, const int \&)}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Evaluates flux on a given face. This function calculates the flux for a given face by considering the current cell number, its neighboring cell corresponding to the face, the face number, and whether the face is a boundary face. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Current\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No} & The number of the current cell. \\
\hline
{\em Neighbour\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No} & The number of the neighboring cell corresponding to the face. \\
\hline
{\em Face\+\_\+\+No} & The face number for which the flux is being calculated. \\
\hline
{\em Is\+\_\+\+Boundary\+\_\+\+Face} & A boolean indicating whether the face is a boundary face. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_u_d_a___integrated___numerical___method_8cpp_source_l00014}{14}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{_c_u_d_a___integrated___numerical___method_8cpp_source}{CUDA\+\_\+\+Integrated\+\_\+\+Numerical\+\_\+\+Method.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{_flux_8h_aa01e7e15e24ab2c77be345cececacfd0_aa01e7e15e24ab2c77be345cececacfd0}\index{Flux.h@{Flux.h}!Condition\_For\_RICCA@{Condition\_For\_RICCA}}
\index{Condition\_For\_RICCA@{Condition\_For\_RICCA}!Flux.h@{Flux.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Condition\_For\_RICCA()}{Condition\_For\_RICCA()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_flux_8h_aa01e7e15e24ab2c77be345cececacfd0_aa01e7e15e24ab2c77be345cececacfd0} 
void Condition\+\_\+\+For\+\_\+\+RICCA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double \&}]{d\+\_\+U}{, }\item[{double \&}]{d\+\_\+F}{, }\item[{double \&}]{Vn\+\_\+L}{, }\item[{double \&}]{Vn\+\_\+R}{, }\item[{double \&}]{dP}{, }\item[{double \&}]{Rho\+\_\+I}{, }\item[{double \&}]{P\+\_\+I}{, }\item[{double \&}]{Alpha}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the Alpha parameter for the RICCA condition based on input variables. 

This function calculates the Alpha parameter, which is used in the RICCA flux computation. It considers the velocity components, pressure differences, and other physical properties to determine the appropriate value of Alpha.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em d\+\_\+U} & Reference to the difference in conserved variables (e.\+g., density, momentum, energy). \\
\hline
{\em d\+\_\+F} & Reference to the difference in flux variables. \\
\hline
{\em Vn\+\_\+L} & Normal velocity on the left side of the interface. \\
\hline
{\em Vn\+\_\+R} & Normal velocity on the right side of the interface. \\
\hline
{\em dP} & Reference to the pressure difference across the interface. \\
\hline
{\em Rho\+\_\+I} & Density at the interface. \\
\hline
{\em P\+\_\+I} & Pressure at the interface. \\
\hline
{\em Alpha} & Reference to the Alpha parameter to be computed.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the pressure difference (dP) is below a small threshold (epsilon), it is set to zero. The function uses the maximum of the absolute values of the normal velocities (Vn\+\_\+L, Vn\+\_\+R) and incorporates a term proportional to the square root of the ratio of pressure to density at the interface, scaled by a constant (gamma).
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Ensure that the input parameters are properly initialized before calling this function. The function assumes that gamma is defined globally or accessible within the scope. 
\end{DoxyWarning}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{_r_i_c_c_a_8cpp_source_l00030}{30}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{_r_i_c_c_a_8cpp_source}{RICCA.\+cpp}}.

\Hypertarget{_flux_8h_a4d08f12e369b293abfbc5536d7ffba7c_a4d08f12e369b293abfbc5536d7ffba7c}\index{Flux.h@{Flux.h}!RICCA@{RICCA}}
\index{RICCA@{RICCA}!Flux.h@{Flux.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RICCA()}{RICCA()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_flux_8h_a4d08f12e369b293abfbc5536d7ffba7c_a4d08f12e369b293abfbc5536d7ffba7c} 
void RICCA (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int \&}]{Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{int \&}]{N\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{const int \&}]{Face\+\_\+\+No}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the dissipative flux for a given cell and face using the RICCA method. 

This function calculates the dissipative flux based on the left and right state variables of a cell interface. It uses the RICCA method to evaluate the flux differences and applies conditions for smooth regions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Cell\+\_\+\+No} & The index of the current cell. \\
\hline
{\em N\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No} & The index of the neighboring cell. \\
\hline
{\em Face\+\_\+\+No} & The index of the face being processed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{_flux_8h_af68071625b590d44a51647290ccc1ee1_af68071625b590d44a51647290ccc1ee1}\index{Flux.h@{Flux.h}!RICCA\_2O@{RICCA\_2O}}
\index{RICCA\_2O@{RICCA\_2O}!Flux.h@{Flux.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RICCA\_2O()}{RICCA\_2O()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_flux_8h_af68071625b590d44a51647290ccc1ee1_af68071625b590d44a51647290ccc1ee1} 
void RICCA\+\_\+2O (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int \&}]{Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{int \&}]{N\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No}{, }\item[{const int \&}]{Face\+\_\+\+No}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the dissipative flux for a given cell and face using the second-\/order RICCA method. 

This function calculates the dissipative flux based on the left and right state variables of a cell interface. It uses the second-\/order RICCA method to evaluate the flux differences and applies conditions for smooth regions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Cell\+\_\+\+No} & The index of the current cell. \\
\hline
{\em N\+\_\+\+Cell\+\_\+\+No} & The index of the neighboring cell. \\
\hline
{\em Face\+\_\+\+No} & The index of the face being processed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{_r_i_c_c_a_8cpp_source_l00135}{135}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{_r_i_c_c_a_8cpp_source}{RICCA.\+cpp}}.
